puis frotez la bouche de la marris d’oiles moistes avec muscillaige de altee et de fenugrec et semence de lin, puis oigne li baile ses mains de ces oiles et de ces muscillaiges;	Then rub the mouth of the woman in labor with moist oil containing musk, fenugreek seeds, and flaxseed powder, then apply these oils and powders to the hands of the attendants.
puis les boute en la marris legierement, puis quiere .i. leu ou elle boute les oncines que soient covenaubles a ceu,	Then put your fingers gently into the woman's vagina, then seek one place where you can grasp the loops that are suitable for this purpose
et pren warde se li enfes est apparilliez qu’il dessende sus son chief;	and be careful that the child is facing downwards so it descends headfirst
si fiche les oncines en ses eulz ou en son col ou en sa bouche ou en som palais ou desoz la barbe ou en la forcele ou pres des costez,	If you hook your fingers in his ears or neck or mouth or palate or under the beard or near the scrotum or close to the sides
et se li dessendemens est sus piez, se li fiche ou poignil et as costes moienes;	and if delivery is on footing, then hook or grasp it by the middle of its sides
et covient qu’il teigne l’oncine a sa main destre, et mette la corbeure entre ses dois de la senestre main, et li boute a tout sa main legierement, et fiche l’oncine en aucun de ces leus que nos avons dit, tant qu’il viegne a la chose vuide;	and it is necessary that he grasp the loop with his right hand, and place the hook between the fingers of his left hand, and insert his hand gently up to the wrist, and grasp the loop at one of these points we have mentioned, until the child emerges empty
et c’est li forme de l’oncine:	And this is the shape of the loop
puis fiche encontre .i. autre oncine, ou le tier se tu en as mestier, si que li estractions soit igalz;	Then insert another loop opposite the first one, or a third if necessary, so that the extraction is even
et puis l’estent igalment en movant d’une part et d’autre, por mues issir, et soit li oncines dentez por mues tenir, si com ci est li forme:	and then pull evenly in both directions, moving back and forth, so that the child may be born more easily, and the loops should be toothed to hold it firmly, as shown here
Et s’il en demoure une partie, si oigne li baile aucuns de ses dois d’oile, et les boute en celle partie, et traie l’autre partie;	And if there is still a part remaining, then let the attendant anoint some of his fingers with oil and insert them into that part, and draw out the other part
et s’il en i demoure point, si met cest oncine ou plus haut leu, et fai ceu tant qu’il s’en isse tout fuers.	and if there is still none remaining, then move this loop higher up and do so until the child is completely born.
Et se l’une mains vient devant l’autre, et il ne puet ramener por l’estreignement,	And if one hand comes before the other and he cannot bring it back to perform the extraction
si covient que tu envoloupes sus .i. drapeil, tant qu’il isse tote;	then you must wrap a cloth around both hands so that they emerge together
puis la cope en la jointure de la plante ou au coute, et ensi covient que tu faices en l’autre main, et as .ij. piés.	Then grasp the baby at the heel joint or the knee, and do likewise with the other hand, using both hands
Et se li chiés de l’enfant est gros et il est estrois en l’issue, ou il ait ou chief aigue assemblee,	And if the hips of the child are large and it is stuck in the outlet or has an acute head coming together,
si covient que tu boute le spatumile espinous entre tes dois, et fent le chief et estrai l’aigue;	It is necessary for you to place the spine-like spatula between your two hands, then press it firmly and draw out the water.
ou tu la ront a l’estrument qui est apelez «almidach», de coi li forme vient avec les estrumens ou chapistre qui est aprés cestui;	or you can roll it with the instrument called "almidach," from which its form comes along with the tools or chapter that follows this one.
et ensi meisme faice se li enfes a grant chief naturelment;	And do likewise if the child has a naturally large head.
et puis traie fuer les osses as tenailles,	"And then grasp the bones with tongs,"
et se li chiés saut fuer et il estraint a la forcele, si soit fendus, tant que li moistors qui est ou pis issue fuer;	"If the hip joint protrudes and is restrained by forceps, it should be cracked open until all moisture in the bone marrow has been expelled;"
et s’elle ne puet issir, si le cope par pieces au mues que tu pues;	"And if it cannot come out, then cut it into pieces with a saw where you are able to."
et s’il est enflez au ventre ou desoz les costez, si covient que tu lou perces tant que li moistors corre.	"If it is swollen in the abdomen or under the ribs, it should be punctured until the moisture flows out."
Et se li enfes est sus ses piez, si est li attraction legiere, et li adrecemens a la bouche de la marris est legier.	"And if the child is on its feet, traction will be light, and the alignment of the mouth of the marrow will be easy."
Et s’il est estrois au ventre ou au pis, si couvient que tu l’estraies a .i. drapeil envoloupeit sus la main;	"And if it is tight in the abdomen or on the bone, then extract it using one cloth wrapped around the hand."
et fent le ventre ou le pis, tant que li moistors qui i est corre;	"Open the abdomen or the bone until the moisture flows out;"
et se li autre membre sont osteit, et li chiez demoure,	"And if the other limbs are dislocated and the hip joint remains in place,"
si boute li baile sa main em parfont de la marris, et le traie jusc’a la bouche de la marris;	"then insert his hand deep into the marrow and draw it up to the mouth of the marrow;"
puis i boute .i. oncine ou ij., et le trai fuer;	"then place one or two fingers inside, and draw it out."
et se li bouche de la marris est retrecie por aposteme chaut qui i est venus, si n’i covient mie travillier,	"And if the mouth of the marrow is constricted due to a hot boil that has formed there, then one should not attempt to manipulate it,"
ains covient amenistrer choses moistes et grasses;	"but rather apply moist and fatty substances;"
et li amenistre emplaustres, et siece en aigue mollifians et amoistans.	"And use poultices, and make compresses with softened and moistening herbs."
Et se li enfes est sus son costeit, et tu le pues mettre igal, si amenistre ceu que nos avons dit en l’enfant vif;	"And if the child is on its side and you are able to place it flat, then apply what we have said for a living child;"
et s’on nen ait pooir, si lou trai fuer par pieces, et n’i laissier rien de la secondine.	"But if one does not have the strength to do so, then draw out the hip joint in pieces and leave no part of the afterbirth behind."
Et quant tu avras ce fait, se li amenistre ceu que nos avons dit ens apostemes chaus que vienent en la marris;	"And once you have done this, if any hot boils appear on the marrow, apply what we have said for treating them;"
et se decorremens de sanc vient, si soit mise en aigue restraignant, et li amenistre autres cures.	"But if bleeding occurs, it should be placed in cold water to restrict it, and other treatments applied."
Et je vis une femme en cui ventre uns enfes avoit esteit mors, puis consut .i. autre sus celui, et refut mors li autres.	"I saw a woman whose child had been bitten in the abdomen by one mouse, then another mouse came and bit the other."
Aprés lonc tens li vint uns apostemes en la boude, et enfla tant qu’il ovrit, et comensa a grant porreture.	"After many days, an abscess formed on her cheekbone and swelled so much that it opened up, causing great pain."
je fui apelez a la cure, et i pensai lonc tens, et ne pot soder li plaie.	"I was called to treat her, but after thinking about it for some time, I could not heal the wound."
Je mis sus emplaustre de fort attraction, et en issit uns os, et aprés aucuns jors uns autres.	"I applied a poultice with strong drawing power and out came one bone, then after a few days another."
Je me mervillai mout, por ceu c’ou ventre n’a point d’os.	"I was greatly amazed at this because the abdomen has no bones."
Si pensai que c’estoit des os d’un enfant mort.	"So I thought it must be the bones of a dead fetus."
Je quis la plaie, et en traï mains os, tant que li femme fut em miglior point;	"I cleaned the wound and drew out many more bones until the woman began to improve;"
et vesquit li femme lonc tens ensi, et issoit adés un poc de bowe dou leu;	"and the woman lived for a long time in this way, with a little blood oozing from the wound sometimes;"
et je n’ai recordeit cest chapistre fuer que por ceu que, quant li maistres trueve une estrainge chose, qu’il i saiche mettre aide.	"And I am recording this chapter here only so that when the master encounters something unusual, he may know how to treat it."
dou ramener la marris a son leu	"on bringing the hip joint back into place"
Ci aprés vient li forme dou pressor, a coi on ewe les livres; et a .ij. tornans as .ij. chiés des .ij. liiens.	Hereafter comes the form of the pressure bandage, with which one wraps the books; and at two turns around the two heads of the two ribs.
Toutevoie, li cornes soit plus subtilz dou restrictoire, et soit fais de ebene ou de bux;	Moreover, let the horns be more subtle in the restraint, and let them be made of ebony or boxwood;
et soit li bouche dou fust .i. doi de large, et li marge des arbres .i. doit, et de lonc une palme et demi;	"And let the mouth of the bellows be two fingers wide, and the edges of the blades one finger wide, and long one and a half palms."
et enmi les .ij. liemens soient dui ajostemens de cest meisme fust, qui soient fermeit en l’un et en l’autre, de demi palme de lonc ou un poc plus;	"And between the two limbs there should be two joints of this same wood, which close in one and open in the other, half a palm long or a little more."
et cist dui ajostement sont bouteit en la bouche de la marris por ovrir quant on torne les .ij. cornes.	"And these two joints are inserted into the mouth of the bellows to open it when one turns the two corners."
Une autre forme, a sa semblance plus subtilz et plus legiere, soit faite de fust de ebene ou de bux, selonc la semblance des tenailles;	"A more refined and lighter form is made of ebony or boxwood, resembling the shape of tongs;"
et ait as .ij. chiés .ij. ajostemens, si com tu vois, d’une palme de lonc, et .ij. dois de large;	"and at both ends it has two joints, each one a palm long and two fingers wide;"
et quant tu vues ovrir la marris a tout l’estrument, si fai seoir la femme sor .i. lit, les piez pendant et les jambes overtes,	"And when you see the bellows open completely with the instrument, have the woman sit on one bed, her feet hanging down and her legs open,"
puis boute les .ij. ajostemens ajostez ensamble en la marris, et tien le chief de l’estrument desoz entre ses cuixes;	"then insert the two joints together into the bellows, and hold the end of the instrument under her thighs;"
puis oevre ta main a tout l’estrument, si com tu as fait as tenailles igalment, selonc la quantiteit que tu vues ovrir la bouche de la marris, tant que li baile faice ceu qu’elle vuet.	"then open your hand on the whole instrument, just like with tongs, according to the amount you see opening the mouth of the bellows, until the ball is done."
Cist estrument sont tuit sormontez, et sont multiplies lor semblances; et quant li mires les ait apareilliez, tant est plus hastans li oevre, et plus haute as homes por lor quantiteit.	"These instruments are all mounted and have multiple similar forms. And when the master has prepared them, he who operates is faster in his work, and higher in esteem among men for his skill."
Si ne despire mie l’estrument que tu ne l’aies apparelliet, car lor necessitez n’est mie escusauble.	"Therefore do not disregard the instrument until you have prepared it, for its usefulness is not negligible."
Quant li secondine est retenue a l’enfantement, si covient que tu comandes a la malaide qu’ele reteigne son alaine, et puis la fai esternuer de condisi, et li estraint tes mains a la bouche et au neis;	"When the midwife is assisting at childbirth, you must command the mother to hold her breath, and then make her sneeze with camphor, and keep your hands over her mouth and nose;"
et s’elle saut per ceu, bien est.	"And if she faints because of this, so much the better."
Se ceu non, si prent .i. pot, et fai .i. pertus ou cuvercle, et i met herbes que puissent ovrir la bouche de la marris, si com calament, rue, anis, camomille, cassialigne et centoire;	"If not, take one pot, make a hole in the lid, and put herbs inside that can open the mouth of the bellows, such as calamint, rue, anise, chamomile, celery seed, and cumin;"
toutes ces herbes, ou aucunes d’eles, soient cuites ou pot en aigue sus le feu; puis met une caine ou pertus dou pot, et l’autre chief en la bouche de la marris,	"all these herbs, or some of them, should be cooked in the pot with water over the fire. Then put one end of a tube into the hole in the pot and the other end into the mouth of the bellows;"
et la teigne tant que li vapors viegne dedens la marris; puis la fai esternuer, si com nos avons dit.	"and hold it there until the vapor comes inside the bellows. Then make her sneeze, as we have said."
Si saut li secondine hastanment.	"If the midwife acts quickly,"
Et s’elle remaint aprés ceste cure, et n’ist mie fuer, si comande a la baile qu’ele moille sa main senestre en oile de sesement ou en muscillaige de altee, et puis la boute en la nature,	"And if the midwife remains afterwards and is not satisfied, command the woman to moisten her left hand with oil of sesame or with white wax, and then put it into the vagina,"
et quiere la secondine; et quant elle l’avra trovee, si la preigne et l’estende poc et poc droitement, si que li marris ne chiece a l’estraction;	"and search for the baby. And when she has found it, take hold of it and stretch it out little by little straight, so that the bellows does not slip out;"
mais la covient movoir legierement a destre et a senestre, et puis traie; si venra et se desaerdra.	"but she must move it gently to the right and left, and then pull it. It will come and be delivered."
Et se li bouche de la marris est jai estrecie, nos avons dit la cure d’esternuer, et de fumigation des herbes;	"And if the mouth of the bellows is too narrow, we have described the treatment of sneezing and the fumigation with herbs;"
et s’elle n’ist de tout ceu que nos avons dit, si garde que tu ne foloies au traire;	"and if she is not helped by any of these things, make sure you do not pull too hard;"
mais il couvient que ceu qui est a la bouche de la marris, que tu le lies a la cuixe de la femme, puis la clisterize d’oignement tetrafarmaçon;	"but the one who is at the mouth of the bellows should tie it to the woman's hip, and then administer an enema with tetrapharmakon oil;"
si la porrira et remettra, et venra fuer; mais toutevoie, quant elle porrist si en vient male odor au stomac et au chief, et blece la malaide.	"This will allow her to push and deliver the baby. However, when she pushes, bad odors may come from her stomach and head, causing discomfort for the woman."
Si covient donques fumigations covenaubles a ceu: aucun des anciens ont esproveit fumigation de cresson et de figues seches.	"Therefore, appropriate fumigations should be applied at this time. Many of the ancients have tried fumigations with watercress and dried figs."
Li forme de l’estrument a coi on fumige la femme a la retenue des flors et de la secondine si est ceste:	"The shape of the instrument used for fumigation of the woman during childbirth and delivery is as follows:"
Et est de voirre semblant a une caine, et met on le chief subtil en la nature, et les chiés larges sus le feu;	"And it resembles a tube made of glass. The narrow end is placed in the vagina, and the wide ends are held over the fire;"
et soit li fumigations sus les charbons, et la teigne tant qu’elle soit gastee, et rencomence une autre.	"and the fumigation should be done with charcoal. Hold it there until it is exhausted, then start another one."
de percier lou fondement	"to pierce the anus"
Maint enfant naissent qui n’ont mie le fondement perciet, ains l’ait estoupeit uns subtilz syfac:	"Many children are born whose anus has not been pierced, but rather obstructed by a subtle membrane;"
si covient donques a la baile qu’ele perce celui syfac a son doit, et ne lou perce mie de spatumile agut, et garse le lacement qu’elle ne le touche;	"therefore the woman should pierce this membrane with her thumb, without touching it with any sharp instrument, and she must take care not to touch it;"
puis met sus lainne moillie en vin et en oile, puis la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	"then apply a compress moistened in wine and oil, and continue the treatment until it is healed."
Et se tu doutes qu’il ne restoupe, si met ou pertus une caine de plonc, et li laisse mains jors, et soit ostee quant li enfes vuet aler en chambres.	"And if you suspect that it has not healed, insert a silver tube into the hole and leave it there for several days. It should be removed when the child is ready to go to its room."
Et aucune fois vient cist estoupemens de soudement de plaie ou d’aposteme; si covient coper celui soudement: si soit curez, si com nos avons dit de la caine de plonc.	"Sometimes this obstruction can be caused by a sudden eruption or boil. In such cases, the eruption should be opened and treated as described for the silver tube."
de la fistule dou fondement	"of a fistula of the anus"
Fistules qui vienent desoz le fondement sont nodation, et groissor que vienent delez lou fondement defuer, ou en l’espaice des .ij. parties,	"Fistulas that come from under the anus are usually nodular and grow larger than those that come beside the anus or in the space between the two buttocks;"
si a une fistule ou plusors; et quant celle nodation est anciene, si aoeuvre, et encort moistor awouse blainche ou subtilz bowe,	"if there is one fistula or more, and when the nodular fistula is old, it opens on its own. However, if it does not open on its own, use a sharp needle or fine knife to incise it;"
et aucune fois sont ces fistule persans; et sont conues par ceu qu’il en ist ou egestion ou ventositeit quant li malaide fait egestion, et par aventure en saut uns vers.	"and sometimes these fistulas are persistent. They can be recognized by the fact that there is a discharge of pus or wind when the person has a bowel movement, and occasionally a worm may emerge;"
Et si a fistules que percent jusc’a la vessie, et jusc’a la moitiet de la verge; et parvienent jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, et jusc’a nout de la kowe.	"And there are fistulas that penetrate all the way to the bladder and halfway up the penis. Some reach as far as the hip joint, and others reach as far as the thighbone."
Et ensi conoist on la fistule persant au fondement, et ne mie persant:	"Thus one can recognize a persistent fistula of the anus that is not persistent;"
et est que tu boutes ton doi indice ou fondement, et boute une aguille subtil d’arain ou de fer en la fistule quant il n’i a tortuositeit.	"and it is necessary to insert your index finger into the anus and then insert a fine needle made of brass or iron into the fistula when there is no curvature;"
Et s’il ait tortuositeit, si i boute une tente de plonc subtil, ou .i. poil de cheval, tant que tu sentes la tente ou le poil a ton doit;	"And if there is curvature, insert a fine silver probe or a horsehair until you feel it with your finger;"
et se tu ne le sens, et il ne vient dou pertus egestion ne ventositeit ne ver, si com nos avons dit:	"and if you do not feel it and there is no discharge of pus, wind, or worm coming from the opening, as we have described;"
saiches qu’elle ne perce mie; si te haste dou curer.	"know that it does not penetrate. Be quick to treat it."
Et quant li fistule est persans jusc’a la vessie ou jusc’a conduit de l’urine, si en saut li urine, et ne puet soudeir par medicines.	"And when a fistula extends all the way to the bladder or the urethra, urine flows out of it and cannot be stopped with medications."
S’elle est percie jusc’a la jointure de la cuixe, si est li tente venans jusc’au leu;	"If it has penetrated as far as the hip joint, the probe will reach there;"
s’il n’i a tortuositeit et li invention de la dolor entor, si est qu’il en ist adés bowe, et n’i vaut medicine ne soudement par oignement;	"if there is no curvature and there is inflammation around it, then it has always been present, and there is no need for medication or cauterization;"
et en ces fistules persans n’a point de cure fuer que labor, et vaniteit des folz mires qui s’en entremettent.	"and in these persistent fistulas, there is no other remedy than hard work, and the vain boasting of foolish physicians who meddle with them."
En celle qui n’est mie persans et n’est mie anciene, a esperance de saniteit par fer, si com j’ai esproveit,	"In one that is not persistent or old, there is hope for healing by means of iron, as I have experienced;"
et est que li malaides gise entre tes mains sus son dos; et li lieve les jambes jusque sus ses cuixes, et ait ses cuixes enclinees a son ventre;	"And the person should lie face down in your hands, with their legs raised up to the hips and the hips tilted towards the abdomen;"
puis boute une tente d’arain, ou de plonc s’il i a tortuositeit, tant que tu saiches ou li tente vient.	"then insert an iron probe or silver if there is curvature, until you know where it emerges."
Se li malaides la sent entor le fondement, si covient que tu i boutes ton doi indice,	If the patient feels it around their fundament, then you must place your two index fingers there.
se sens adonques que li tente l’ait perciet; et soit descoverte ou tu sens entre ton doit le syfac ou la char, adonques saiches qu’elle est persans;	Next, feel if the tendon has pierced through; and whether it is exposed or you can feel between your fingers skin or flesh, then know that it has pierced.
si n’i travillier mie c’on ne la puet saner.	If one does not work on it, one cannot heal it.
On dist toutevoie c’on em puet bien saner aucuns, mais ce avient poc;	It is always said that some can be healed well, but this happens rarely;
et li aide c’on i fait, si est c’on eschaufe le cautere subtil selonc la largesce de la fistule, si com il est devant dit;	"and the aid that is done there, if it is done, then heat the cautery thinly according to the width of the fistula, as it is said before."
et le boute tout chaut en la fistule, tant qu’il viegne delez le fondement; et faice ceu .ij. fois ou .iij., tant que tu saiches que ces chars fautrees soient arses, qui sont semblant a une penne d’oiseil;	"And push it all hot into the fistula until it reaches the fundament; and do this two or three times, until you know that these broken veins have been burned, which resemble an eagle's feather."
et puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre, tant que celle chars isse fuer, puis le cure d’oignement enjanrant char et soudant.	"And then, the dressing of wet cloths is applied until that broken vein comes out; then the application of ointment between flesh and skin."
S’il est ensi sanez, c’est bien. Se ceu, nom autrement ne puet estre sanez;	"If it is thus healed, that's good. But if not, there is no other way to heal it:"
et se li tente entre, et ne perce jusc’au doit qui est ou fondement, et a entre ton doi et la tente une coverture espesse de char ou de syfac, et tu vois la fistule a ceu qui enseut la coverture dou keur;	"And if the tent enters and does not reach to the thumb which is at the fundament, and between your two fingers there is a thick covering of flesh or skin, and you see the fistula coming out from under this covering near the heart:"
si le cope des l’encomencement de la fistule, et boute adés avant la tente, et pues le cautere aprés, tant qu’il viegne au chief de la tente;	"then cut through the beginning of the fistula, and push the tent forward again, and then apply the cautery until it reaches the tip of the tent."
et sera delivré li tente, et cherra; puis mondefie celles chars fautrees que semblent une penne d’oisel, et n’en remaigne niant.	"And thus the tent will be delivered and fall away; then burn those broken veins which resemble an eagle's feather, and nothing will remain."
Et si li sans te vaint, et cort entre toi et l’uevre, si le cauterize de feu ou de medicine ague.	"If the skin becomes inflamed, and cracks between you and the wound, then cauterize it with fire or strong medicine."
Car li cauteres de feu assemble .ij. bones choses: c’est a savoir, l’arsure de ces chars ajostees, et l’esteinchement de sanc et la sechor de la moistor;	"For the cautery of fire accomplishes two things: namely, it burns those broken veins together and stops the flow of blood and dries up the moisture."
puis le cure de tentes moillies em burre ou en choz broiez, tant que li leus giete bowe, et isse fuer li chars arse en la bowe;	"then apply dressings moistened with hot water or crushed herbs until the place becomes soft and the burned vein comes out from the flesh;"
puis cure la plaie des oignemens soudans enjanrans dure char, et sont les medicines seches.	"then dress the wound with healing ointments that are applied between hard flesh, and these are dried medicines."
Car quant il est restoree, si est sanee et ne revient mie.	"For when it is thus restored, it will be healed and not return again."
Et se fistule vient jusc’a parfont dou fondement, et est esloigniez dou cors, se li boute ton doi ou fondement, et enquier ceu.	"And if the fistula comes right up from the fundament but is distant from the body, push your thumb into the fundament and feel with it."
Se tu sens la tente, et entre .ij. est li toile ou li syfac ou chars, ou il est pres a percier, si n’i ait fuers que voie de fiance et d’esperance, par l’aministrement de l’une des .iii. manieres:	"If you feel the tent with your thumb and there are two layers between it – skin or flesh – where it is about to burst, then there should be no fear of danger or despair, for there are three ways to manage this:"
ou tu le cauterizes si com nos avons dit, ou tu le cope jusc’a fons, ou se tu pues si i met tentes et cure si com premier;	"either you cauterize it as we have described, or cut through it completely until it reaches the bottom, or if you can push a tent into it and dress it as before."
et n’aler mie trop em parfont, que tu ne coper le tenement qui tient le fondement, et viegne li egestions par lai sens volenteit;	"but do not go too deep lest you cut the tissue that supports the fundament, so that evacuations can pass without difficulty;"
puis le cure, si com nos avons dit;	"then dress it as we have described;"
par aventure si sera sanez, ou tu esloigne celle coverture et la munde puis qu’elle est copee delez lou fondement, ou par tente ou par autre estrument apointé;	"perhaps it will then be healed, or you can remove that covering and clean it after it has been cut near the fundament with a tent or another pointed instrument;"
puis mondefie cele char fautree qui est en la plaie, tant com tu pues;	"then burn the broken veins in the wound as much as possible;"
puis estudie a restorer la plaie, et a demorer la fistule en la partie defuers le fondement: si iert plus legiere chose au malaide.	"then endeavor to restore the wound and keep the fistula away from the fundament: this will be easier for the patient."
Et aucune fois sont fistules selonc ceste maniere: et est quant tu boutes la tente en la fistule, et elle est ou costeit dou fondement delez lou cuir desus,	"And there are sometimes fistulas of this kind: when you push the tent into the fistula and it is located on the side of the fundament near the skin above;"
si pren une tente percie au chief selonc ceste forme:	"then take a tent with a hole at its tip like this:"
Et i boute .i. fil tort en .ij., et boute la tente a tout le fil en la fistule tant qu’il soit au chief.	"And thread two turns of thread onto it, then insert the tent all the way down to its tip into the fistula."
S’elle est persans en la marge dou fondement dedens, adonc estrai lou fil de celui pertus, ensi que tu boutes ton doi ou fondement;	"If it passes through the margin of the fundament inside, then pull out the thread from that hole so that you can insert your thumb into the fundament;"
et trai le chief dou fil, et assemble les .ij. chiés ensamble, et estraint l’un a l’autre, et le laisse .i. jor ou .ij.;	"then pull on the end of the thread and draw the two holes together, tying them tightly to each other, and leave it in place for one or two days;"
et le restraint aucune fois, tant que li filz cope ces chars que sont entre dous, et chiecent;	"and tie it again if necessary until the thread cuts through those veins that are between them and they close up;"
puis cure la plaie tant qu’elle soit soudee et sanee.	"then dress the wound until it is healed."
Se li fistule ne perce, si la fai percier en toutes les manieres que tu pues, s’ele n’est trop em parfont.	"If the fistula does not open on its own, then make an incision in any way that you can, if it is not too deep."
Car il ne covient mie faire por le lacement coper si em parfont, et puis le cure, si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez.	"For one should not cut too deeply for the sake of making a hole and then dress it as we have described until it is healed."
Li forme dou spatumile espinous dont on fent la fistule si est mout agus d’une, part et trenchans;	"The shape of the spinal comb used to open a fistula is most often pointed and cutting;"
et d’autre part non, por ceu c’on ne cope mie ceu c’on ne doit mie copeir, si com tu vois ci:	"and on the other hand, it should not be wide so that one does not cut what ought not to be cut, as you can see here:"
des emorroydes	"hemorrhoids"
Emorrydes sont selonc ij. manieres: ou elles sont dedens le fondement, ausi com grain de resin, et s’en i a petites et grans, et en cort adés sanc,	"There are two kinds of hemorrhoids: those that are inside the fundament, like grains of resin, and there can be small or large ones. Sometimes they bleed outside;"
et s’en i a une ou plusors, et sont defuer le fondement et au chief dou fondement; mais celles qui sont defuer si ont poc de moistor,	"and there is one or more of them, and they are located outside the fundament at its tip. But those that are outside have less moisture;"
et encort adés ou un poc d’aigue citrine ou un poc de sanc, et ont la color dou cors;	"and they are usually covered with a little yellow mucus or blood, and they have the color of skin;"
et li cure de ces qui les ont dedens le fondement, si est que tu comandes au malaide qu’il s’espreigne por aleir en chambres, tant que li fondemens li isse fuer, et c’aperent li filz;	"The treatment for those who have hemorrhoids inside the fundament is to tell the patient to strain while going to the privy until the fundament protrudes and the veins are emptied;"
si te haste, et le pent as tenailles, ou tu le tien a ton ungle, puis le cope en ses racines;	"then act quickly, take hold of it with forceps or your fingernail, then cut through its root;"
et se li uncine ne les pueent tenir por ses moistors, si les prent a .i. drapeil, ou a couton, ou d’une piece de chamelot;	"And if the nails cannot hold them due to their moisture, then take them with a cloth or cotton or a piece of linen;"
et les estrai a tes dois, puis les cope, et poudre desus aucunes chaudes poudres que soient en leu de cautere;	"then pull them out with your thumbs, cut them off and apply some warm powders instead of cauterizing;"
ou tu les cauterize si com il est dit ou chapistre de cautere, puis les cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez;	"or cauterize them as is described in the chapter on cautery, then treat them with other remedies until they are healed."
et se li fondemens ne puet issir, si clisterize le malaide de clistere mordant et aspre por laver ceu qui est ou fondement, si qu’il puist issir apertement;	"And if the fundament cannot protrude, then administer a strong and sharp enema to wash out what is inside the fundament so that it can come out openly;"
cant li malaides se preint, et se li fil sont fuer dou fondement, si est li cure legiere;	"when the patient strains, if the veins are protruding from the fundament, then treatment will be easy;"
et est que tu les preignes a ton ungle ou as tenailles, et les cope, puis les cure si com nos avons dit, tant qu’il soit sanez, et qu’il redoute l’incision par fer.	"And it is necessary to take hold of them with your fingernail or forceps and cut them off, then treat them as we have described until they are healed, and the patient fears being cut by a knife."
Si covient que tu amenistre la costure selonc ceste maniere: pren .i. fil tort, et le boute en une aguille, et puis trai le fil au desus et fai percier l’aguille d’autre part, et torne les .ij. chiez dou fil desoz l’aguille,	"The stitch must be made in this way: take a thread and pass it through a needle, then pull the thread upwards and pierce the needle from below, and turn both ends of the thread down under the needle;"
et si soit dou large; et estraint le fil forment, puis noe le fil, et estrai l’aguille, et fai ensi de toz les autres, et en laisse .i. por corre la superfluiteit dou sanc;	"and tie it tightly, then knot the thread and remove the needle, and do the same for all the others, leaving one loose to drain any excess blood;"
puis met sus le fondement .i. drapeil moilliet en oile roset ou en cerote, et met sus le fondement, et comande au malaide k’il repose;	"then place a warm cloth moistened with rose oil or wax on the fundament and tell the patient to rest;"
et puis le laisse tant qu’il chiecent, et quant il seront cheut, si les cure d’oignement et d’autre cure, tant qu’il soit sanez.	"And then leave it alone until they fall out, and when they do, treat them with ointment and other remedies until they are healed."
dou sechement dou fiens ou fondement	"on the drying of fistulas in the fundament"
Maintes fois avient sechement de fiens en l’intestine, et par constrignement de nature, et quant li maladie est vielle et medicine n’i vaut.	"Sometimes there is a drying up of fistulas in the intestines due to constriction of nature, and when the disease is old and medicine no longer helps;"
Si covient que tu reses a la point d’un spatumile ou a ton ungle l’escorce desus, qui ne le laisse a moistir;	"It is necessary that you scrape off with the tip of a scalpel or your fingernail the skin above it which might otherwise become moist;"
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sodez si com il covient;	"then treat it until it is dry as needed;"
et s’il ne puet soder, si rencomence la rasure plus fort que devant, tant qu’il saine mout, et soit escorchiez;	"And if it cannot be dried up, then scrape more vigorously until it heals completely and is scraped raw;"
puis le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	then heal until he is well
dou fremit	fever
Formice est une petite apparance fautree antor le cors, et va mout em parfont;	An ant is a small animal that lives near the body and moves very quickly;
et aucune fois la trueve li frois, et le sent on ausi comme mort de fremit, et vient en tout le cors, et plus as mains que autre part.	And sometimes it finds the bone, and one feels it like death from shivering, and it comes throughout the body, but more in the hands than elsewhere.
Et li cure si est que tu pren une cainne d’une penne d’oie, ou une penne de vultul fort, et met celle caine sus le fremit, tant que li cercles porpreigne le fremit tot entor;	And the cure for this is that you take a goose feather quill or a strong turkey feather quill, and place it on the shivering until the circle around it encloses the entire shivering.
puis torne ta main a tout la cainne tant que tu copes tout entor le fremit, et le met em parfont, et esraiche le fremit de ses racines.	Then turn your hand around the quill so that you encircle the entire shivering and drive it deep in, and crush its roots.
Et se tu vues, si fai ceu d’une caine d’arain ou de fer selonc ceste forme, et soit subtilz desoz et traians desus:	"And if you see this, do so with a cane of brass or iron according to this form, and let it be thin underneath and pointed above:"
ne mie perciet, por mues tenir au doi, et mues presser Et se tu vues, si cauterize lou fremit, si com il est devant ou chapistre de cautere.	"However, do not pierce too deeply to hold the two together and apply pressure. And if you see this, cauterize the trembling, as it is said in front or in the chapter on cautery."
de la forme dou clistere	"of the form of the enema"
Aucune fois fait on clistere d’argent ou d’archaut, ou d’arain fondut ou mailliet; et aucune fois fait on de ces estrumens petis et grans, selonc ces a cui il sont amenistrez.	"No one ever makes an enema of silver or copper, or melted brass or lead; and no one ever makes them of these small and large instruments, according to which they are ordered."
Cil donques c’on amenistre en la cure des enfans et qui sont foible et dolorous, sont petis.	"Therefore, those that should be used in the treatment of children and those who are weak and painful are small."
Li forme dou clistere petit et grant si est desus large, ou li ventres est liiez selonc ceste maniere:	"The form of the small and large enema is as follows, where the belly is tied according to this manner:"
et i ait une desevrance ou li ventres soit liiez, si com tu vois, et li chiez soit dedens perciez; et ait a l’un des costez .ij. pertus, et en l’autre .i.;	"And there should be an opening where the belly is tied, as you see here, and the feces inside should be pierced; and it should have two holes on one side and one on the other."
et soit li ventres ou om met les medicines d’une vessie de beste ou de parchemin, et soit perciez tout entor de menus pertus,	"And let the belly where one puts the medications be a beast's bladder or parchment, and let it be pierced all around with small holes,"
et ait entre chescun pertus .i. doit d’espaice, puis boute en ces pertus .i. fil fort de fil crut tort en .x. ou enqui entor, et assemble le ventre si com est une chievre;	"And let there be between each hole one grain of spice, then put in these holes one strong thread of thick twisted cotton around ten or eleven times, and fasten the belly like a goat."
et quant li medicine est dedens, si la lie a l’estrument devant d’un fil fort, puis clisterize; et c’est li forme dou cercle:	"And when the medication is inside, tie it to the instrument before with a strong thread, then perform the enema; and this is the form of the circle:"
Et soit li medicine ne trop chaude ne trop froide, et oint le chief dou clistere d’oile ou d’aubun d’uef, ou de semblant chose, puis le boute ens legierement;	"And let the medication not be too hot nor too cold, and grease the head of the enema with oil or dough made from an egg white, or something similar, then put it in gently."
puis l’espreigne li ministres a ses .ij. mains ensamble, tant qu’il soit toz vuis, puis estrai lou clistere, et lieve li malaides ses jambes a la paroit,	"Then the minister squeezes it with both hands together until it is all squeezed out, then remove the enema and have the patient raise their legs at the edge of the bed,"
et se li medicine vuet issir, si la teigne tant com il puet; et s’il dort une nuit atot, si est plus grans aide.	"and if the medication wants to come out, then tie it as much as you can; and if he sleeps all night like that, it is more helpful."
Et se tu le clisterizes em maladie de decorrement de ventre, et li medicine se haste d’issir, si le rencomence tant qu’il soit sanez.	"And if you perform an enema on someone with diarrhea and the medication comes out quickly, then start it again until it is finished."
Et se li emorroide sont ou fondement, ou aposteme, si soit li clistere ausi subtilz com por .i. enfant;	"And if the hemorrhoids are in the fundament or have an ulcer, let the enema be as subtle as for a one-year-old child;"
et c’est li forme dou clistere subtil sus coi li cuir soit estraint:	"and this is the form of the subtle enema on which the skin should be strained:"
des plaies	"wounds."
Nos avons jai dit en la division la cure des plaies; or vos dirons les cures de mains et de medicine, selonc l’acomplissement.	"We have already spoken in the division about the treatment of wounds; now we will tell you about the treatments for hands and medications, according to their completion."
Je dis que les plaies sont diverses selonc ceu qu’elles sont faites, et selonc les leus ou les plaies sont faites, et de coi elles sont faites.	"I say that wounds are diverse according to how they are made, and according to where the wounds are made, and what they are made from."
Les choses par coi plaies sont faites sont par gitement de piere, et taille d’espee et de couteil, ou de lance ou de fust ou de siette, ou de semblans choses;	"The things by which wounds are made are: blows with stones, cuts with swords and knives or lances, clubs, sticks, or similar objects;"
ou que sont faites selonc les leus dou cors, si com plaie que chiet sus le col, ou sus le chief, ou le peis, ou le ventre, ou le foie, et semblans membres;	"or those that are made according to the locations on the body, such as wounds that fall on the neck, head, face, belly, liver, and similar members;"
et je vos dirai la cure de chescune plaie, et encomencerai as plaies dou chief simples, car li remenbrance venra en son chapistre.	"And I will tell you the treatment for each wound, and I will begin with simple head wounds, for the memory will come in its chapter."
Je dis que quant simple plaie vient ou chief, et li os n’est brisiez, si pren garde se c’est de gitement de piere ou de semblans choses, et li cuir est toutevoie rompus et est li plaie grans,	"I say that when a simple wound comes to the head and the bone is not broken, take care if it was caused by a blow with stones or similar objects, and if the skin is completely torn and the wound is large,"
et tu doutes levement d’aposteme chaut: si le fai tantost sainier de la cephalique meismement s’il vient poc de sanc de la plaie, et soit li sainie au contraire de la partie navree;	"and quickly clean the hot ulcer: do it gently with the cephalic balm even if there is a little blood coming from the wound, and let the ointment be applied on the opposite side of the wounded part;"
et eschuisse li malaides repletion de vin et de viandes grosses.	"and keep the patient from overeating wine and fatty foods."
Et s’il ne vuet sainier, si soit amenuisie sa viande, et ne boive point de vin, ne ne menjuce point de char;	"And if it does not want to be cleaned, then soften its flesh, and do not let it drink wine or eat meat;"
et met sor la plaie, se apostemes chaus i vient, coton moilliet en oile roset soulement, ou en vin stiptice;	"and put on the wound, if hot ulcers come, cotton soaked in rose oil only, or in styptic wine;"
et s’il n’i a aposteme chaut, si met sus la plaie, s’elle est fresche a tout son sanc, et elle n’est muee par l’air, poudre, que je dirai un poc ci aprés;	"And if there are no hot ulcers, put on the wound powder that I will tell you about later, if it is fresh with all its blood and has not been moved by the air."
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucuns oignemens, tant qu’il soit sanez.	"And if the air has moved it, put on some ointments until it is healed."
Et se li plaie est grans si com de tailleure d’espee et de semblans, et les levres ne se pueent assembler par tentes, si les assemble par cousture, si com je dirai as plaies dou ventre, de la costure.	"And if the wound is large, like a cut from a sword or similar objects, and the lips cannot be brought together by force, then bring them together by stitching, as I will tell you about in the treatment of abdominal wounds."
Se li plaie est descoverte de l’os, et pent, et ne tient mais que a un poc, si le cope; puis cure la plaie de medicine, et restoure char dure en leu de cuir,	"If the wound is open to the bone and hangs down and only holds on by a little bit, then cut it off. Then treat the wound with medication and replace hard flesh in place of skin."
et comande au malaide a mengier grosses viandes, si com testes et froment cuit, ausi com poulz, et semblans choses.	"and order the patient to eat fatty foods, such as testicles and cooked wheat, as well as poultry and similar things."
Et se tu trueves ou cuir porriture, et il n’aert a l’os, si cope lou porrit tot, et giete fuer, puis le cure;	"And if you find rottenness in the skin but not to the bone, then cut out all the rotting flesh and throw it away, then treat the wound;"
et se il ait artere en la plaie ou voine, dont sans cort, et il ne puet estainchier par medicines, si quier l’artere, et se tu la trueves desloie, si la lie d’un fil;	"And if there is an artery in the wound that bleeds without clotting and it cannot be stopped with medications, then tie off the artery. And if you find it dislocated, then secure it with a thread."
et se ceu ne profite mie, si la cauterize.	"And if that does not help, then cauterize it."
Et se ces plaies sont petites et simples, si est li cure legiere: et est que tu mettes ens ceste poudre qui soude ainsois que li ars l’ait muee.	"And if these wounds are small and simple, the treatment is easy: you should put in this powder that welds before the air has moved it."
Et li maniere de la poudre si est: pren encens une partie; sanc de dragon .ij. parties; chalz vive .iij. parties, et le poudre subtilment,	"And the way to make the powder is: take incense in one part; dragon's blood, two parts; quicklime, three parts, and grind it finely;"
et emple la plaie, et l’estraint forment, tant qu’elle s’aerse bien et se joigne a tout son sanc;	"and fill the wound with it, and bind it tightly until it is well aired and joined together with all its blood;"
et puis la lie bien, et la laisse sens desliier, s’elle n’enfle; car on n’oste la madicine tant qu’ele soit sanee.	"then tie it up well, and do not untie it if it does not swell, because the medication should not be removed until the wound is healed."
Et aucune fois fait on ceu de chalz soulement, quant on n’ait l’encens ne lou sanc de dragon, mais que li ars n’ait muee la plaie.	"Sometimes this can also be done with quicklime alone when incense and dragon's blood are not available, but only if the air has not moved the wound."
Et se li ars ait mueit la plaie, meismement en esteit, si n’i met om mie ceste poudre;	"And if the air has moved the wound, especially in summer, do not put this powder on it at all;"
mais met sus aucuns oignemens digestis, ou poulz de farine d’orge faites d’aigue et de miel, tant qu’ele giete bowe;	"but put on digested ointments or poultices made from barley flour and water and honey until it sweats."
puis le cure d’autres cures tant qu’il soit sanez.	"Then treat it with other treatments until it is healed."
Et se li brisure d’os vient avec la plaie, et elle est petite, si l’estrai as pinceures subtilz;	"And if there is a bone fracture along with the wound and it is small, then extract it with fine forceps;"
et je vos dirai ci aprés les brisures dou chief.	"I will tell you about fractures of the head later on."
de la plaie dou col	"Of the wound on the neck"
Se plaie vient ou col et elle est simple, si n’a point de difference entre li et celi dou chief, mais se li ners dou col ou li artere est copee.	"If a wound comes to the neck and it is simple, there is no difference between it and one on the head, except when the nerve of the neck or an artery is cut."
Se c’est li ners, si n’i a autre engien que laissier la cure, et n’i mettre nulle chose restraignant, car il nuit as ners et les fait retraire;	"If it's a nerve, there is no other remedy than to leave it alone and not put anything constricting on it because that harms the nerves and makes them retreat;"
et ne mettre sus la plaie rien froit, car li substance des ners est froide, et li continuation d’aus si est avec le cerveil, qui est li plus haus membres;	"and do not put anything cold on the wound because nerve tissue is cold and their continuity is with the brain, which is the highest member;"
mais soit li medicine souez, si com chalz lavee en aigue douce, et mellee avec oile roset, et cucie lavee ausi en aigue douce,	"but let the medication be warm, like hot water mixed with sweet oil and honey, also washed in hot water;"
et autres pieres de mine selonc ceste maniere, et oignemens moistes.	"and other mines of stone according to this manner, and moist anointments."
Et se li plaie est grans, si la cout et lie de bendes, puis la cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	"And if the wound is large, then stitch it up with thread and bind it with bandages until it heals."
Et se les plaies sont parfondes et ele est chevee et pleinne de bowe, si la perce ou plus bas leu;	"And if the wounds are deep and full of infection and bowels, then pierce them below or further down,"
et se li artere est copee, et decorremens de sanc en vient, si la desoivre, et la loie, et la cauterize se mestier est;	"and if the artery is cut and there is a flow of blood coming out, then tie it off, ligate it, and cauterize it if necessary;"
et se li espinee de la gorge est copee, ou li keurs, et li conduiz est gardez, par coi la viande va,	"And if the spine or heart is cut and the vessels are preserved so that the flesh remains alive,"
si cout le keur sus la cainne de la gorge, et ne touchier la gorge mais la remet selonc sa figure naturel;	"then stitch up the heart along the side of the neck, without touching the throat but putting it back into its natural shape."
et puis l’estrain avenanment, et le laisse aucuns jors, puis le cure d’oignemens desechans tant qu’il soit sanez;	"and then bind it tightly and leave it for a few days before curing it with drying ointments until it heals."
et se li plaie a fait empression en l’os, si la quier;	"And if the wound has caused an impression on the bone, remove it;"
et s’il i a pieces d’os, si les trai fuers toz se tu pues, et ces que tu ne pues avoir, si laisse tant que li plaie porrisse,	"and if there are pieces of bone, draw out those that you can easily reach; those that you cannot have removed, leave them alone until the wound becomes gangrenous,"
et soit desevree et aligie li issue;	"and remove and ligate any discharge;"
et se li plaie est fresche, si poudre sus la poudre que j’ai dit.	"And if the wound is fresh, then sprinkle on it the powder that I have mentioned."
Et s’il a en la plaie os et il i a fistule, si la cure ensi com j’ai dit en son chapistre.	"And if there are bones in the wound and there is a fistula, cure it as I have said in its chapter."
de la plaie de lance ou de coutel	"Regarding wounds from spears or daggers,"
Se c’est cop de lance ou de coutel, et li plaie est parfonde, si regarde se de la plaie saut ventositez cant li malaides alainne: saiches adonques que li plaie est mortelz;	"If it's a wound from a spear or dagger and the wound is deep, observe whether there are any signs of wind escaping from the wound where the patient breathes: then know that the wound is mortal."
et s’elle n’est parfonde, et elle est fresche a tout son sanc, si n’i mettre mie a la premiere houre la poudre, ne ne la liier mie por le sanc que ne demorse em parfont,	"But if it's not deep and the wound is fresh with all its blood, don't put any powder on it or tie it at first hour so that the blood doesn't sink in too deep,"
et reviegne au cuer, et ocie lou malaide;	"and let it flow towards the heart, causing death to the patient;"
mais i met oignement atractif, et le lie .ij. fois le jor;	"But apply an attracting ointment and tie it twice a day;"
et se tu n’as oignement, si met en la plaie viel coton por succier fuers la moistor,	"And if you don't have any ointment, put some old cotton in the wound to suck out the moisture."
et fai dormir le malaide sus la plaie .iij. jors, ou .iiij., ou plusors;	"And make the patient lie on their side for 3 days or 4 days or more;"
si n’i venra mie spasme, ne tremor male de cuer n’es traingnemens d’alainne;	"So that there will be no spasm, nor trembling of the heart, nor coughing."
et quant tu vois les bones dispositions, si saiches que li plaie est sauve.	"And when you see these good signs, know that the wound is saved."
Cure la donques de tentes et d’autres cures, tant qu’il soit sanez;	"So cure it then with dressings and other treatments until it heals;"
et s’elle ne puet saner, et oevre, adés saiches que il i a fistule; si la cure si com on doit.	"And if it cannot heal and opens up again, know that there is a fistula present; so treat it as it should be treated."
Et se li plaie est d’incision d’espee ou de coutel, et elle est simple, ou pis ou au dos, si la cure de ceu qui est devant;	"And if the wound is an incision from a sword or dagger, whether it's simple, deep, or on the back, treat it as those that are on the front;"
s’elle est grans, de cousture; et s’elle est petite, de poudre, et s’elle est empressee en l’os, et en a copeit pieces, si quier la plaie, et les trai fuers s’il sont desevrez;	"If it's large, stitch it up; if it's small, sprinkle powder on it. And if it's close to the bone and has cut off pieces of flesh, remove the wound and draw out any discharge if they are visible;"
et s’il ne sont desevrez, si laisse porrir la plaie, si aligera li estractions;	"And if they are not visible, let the wound gangrene and then ligate the drainage."
et des autres plaies as autres membres est li jugemens si com nos avons dit.	"And the treatment for wounds on other limbs is judged in the same way as we have said."
dou derrompement dou ventre	"Regarding rupture of the abdomen"
Li derompemens dou ventre est grans et moiens et petis;	"The ruptures of the abdomen are large, medium, and small;"
de la grant plaie saut aucune fois li intestine, ou li ners des intestines, par coi li intromission d’aus;	"A large rupture can sometimes cause the intestines or the nerves of the intestines to protrude through it;"
et li costure est plus malaisie, et aucune fois vaut pis li petite plaie que li grans,	"And stitching is more difficult, and sometimes a small rupture is worse than a large one,"
por ceu c’on remet plus a poinnes les intestines en, s’on ne les i remet de chaut en chaut;	Because when one resets it more often, the intestines are put back in place little by little;
por ce que li intestine enflent tantost qu’il sentent le froit, si rentrent plus a poinnes,	Because the intestines swell up so much that they feel cold, so they cannot be reset.
et por ceu vaut mues li moieinne plaie, por ceu c’on ramoine mues l’intestine a son leu que as autres .ij.	And therefore it is necessary to move the wounded flesh, so that one may reset the intestines to their place like the others.
Et saiches que li routure dou ventre est selonc .iiij. manieres:	And you should know that intestinal rupture occurs in four ways
les .ij. costures communes avienent en la costure dou ventre,	The two common sutures occur in the abdominal suture,
et li costure des autres plaies dou cors et .ij. autres costures propres sont communes as autres plaies;	"And the stitching of other wounds of the body, two other stitches are common for other wounds;".
et toutevoie elles sont plus propres avec la costure dou ventre, et je dirai une chescune et declairerai.	"However, they are more appropriate with abdominal suturing, and I will mention each one and explain."
Je di que quant li plaie est petite, et aucune chose de l’intestine ist fuer,	"I say that when the wound is small and no part of the intestine has come out,"
et griés chose est dou remettre, ceu est par l’une des .ij. manieres:	"and if it is necessary to replace it, this is done in one of two ways:"
ou por la petitece de la plaie, si com nos avons dit,	"or because the wound is small, as we have said,"
ou por ce que li intestine est enflez por le froit.	"or because the intestine is swollen with cold."
Et quant il est frois, eschaufez lou en teil maniere:	"And when it is cold, heat it in this manner:"
moillie une esponge ou .i. mol drapeil en aigue tede soulement,	"Soak a sponge or one piece of cloth in hot water only,"
ou tu cuis en aigue squinant et cipre et spique,	"or cook it in boiling water with vinegar and cumin,"
et arose l’intestine tant que li enfleure soit ostee;	"and raise the intestine until the swelling has gone away;"
et aucune fois fait ce vins restraingnans, et est muedre que awe soule por desenfler.	"And sometimes this wine astringent is made, and it is useful to use for desswelling."
Et quant tu vois l’enfleure departir, si amoiste l’intestine d’aigue ou altee et malves soient cuites,	"And when you see the swelling diminish, then mix the intestine with water or with salt water in which herbs have been cooked,"
car par ceu est aligie li entree a poc de chose;	"because by this method the entrance to the wound is almost closed;"
et s’il n’i puet entrer, si fent un poc la plaie a l’estrument de coi on cope les emorroydes;	"And if it cannot enter, then open the wound a little with an instrument used for cutting hemorrhoids;"
et li premiere cure est muedre que li taille,	"and the first treatment is useful to make the cut;"
que nus n’i doit taillier sens grant necessiteit n’i ait;	"That no one should cut without great necessity being present;"
et c’est li estrumens por le fendre:	"And this is the instrument for splitting it open:"
si trenche dedens en la corbeure et defuer non, et vez ci la forme:	"So cut into the curve and do not go too deep, and here is its shape:"
Et quant li plaie est enlargie, et li intestine saut fuer,	"And when the wound has become enlarged and the intestine has come out,"
si le remet arer selonc la forme naturel en son leu propre,	"then put it back in place according to its natural form in its proper place,"
se tu en as pooir, car ce vaut mues.	"If you are able to do so, for this is most useful."
Quant li plaie est large, et elle est en la partie desoz lou ventre,	"When the wound is large and it is located below the belly,"
si covient que tu faices gesir lou malaide sus son dos,	"It is necessary that you make the sick person lie on his back,"
et met ses jambes plus haut que son chief;	"And put his legs higher than his head;"
et s’elle est en la partie desoz le ventre,	"And if it is located below the belly,"
si met le chief et le pis plus haut que les parties desoz,	"then put the head and chest higher than the parts below."
et ausi se li routure dou ventre est en l’une des .ij. parties	"And also, if the rupture of the belly is in one of the two parts,"
si met t’entente en ceu que li partie navree soit plus haute que li autre;	"then take care that the injured part is higher than the other;"
et ensi covient amenistrer ceu que je dis en plaies grans et moienes.	"And thus it is necessary to arrange what I say in large and moderate wounds."
Es plaies petites met ceu que t’est apparilliet,	"In small wounds, put what you are equipped with,"
puis aies entre tes mains .i. ministre pitous ki teigne toute la routure a sa main,	"then have between your hands one gentle minister who will pull all the rupture with his hand,"
et assemble les levres;	"And join the lips;"
et c’est la maniere commune de costures,	"This is the common manner of stitching."
et est que tu preignes une aguille ou plusors, selonc la quantiteit de la largesce de la plaie,	"And it is necessary that you take one needle or several, according to the quantity of the width of the wound,"
puis laisse des le chief de la plaie .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une aguille ou il ait .i. boin fil fort;	Then leave at the head of the wound two threads of spice, and insert a needle with one good strong thread attached.
et perce les .ij. chiés dou cuir avec les .ij. chiés dou siphac,	And pierce the two holes in the skin with the two holes in the syringe,
qui est desoz le cuir dedens, tant que tu la faices percier de celle partie,	"Which is underneath the skin inside, so that you make it pierce from that part,"
et assemble les .ij. chief dou siphac les .iiij. ensamble;	"And join the two heads of the siphac together with the four."
puis l’estrain d’un fil double entor l’aguille de .ij. pars,	"Then tie a doubled thread around the needle on both sides,"
puis assemble les .ij. chiés de la plaie avenanment,	"Then join the two heads of the wound together,"
et puis laisse .i. doi d’espaice, et i fiche une autre aguille;	"And then leave one finger's width, and stick in another needle;"
puis la lie dou fil si com tu as fait la premiere aguille,	"then tie the thread like you did for the first needle,"
et ne cesser de ceu faire selonc ceu que tu as mestier des aguilles,	"And continue doing this according to how many needles you need."
tant que toute li plaie soit restrainte;	Until the entire wound is closed.
et soient les aguilles moienes, entre subtilz et grosses,	"And let the needles be of medium size, neither too fine nor too coarse,"
car les aguilles subtilz copent toute la char, et les trop grosses si ne pueent mie bien entrer:	For thin needles cut all the flesh, and thick ones cannot go in well enough:"
por ceu covient qu’elles soient moienes;	Therefore they must be medium-sized.
et ne covient mie bouter les aguilles trop au defuer de la char et dou cuir,	And it is not necessary to put the needles too deep into the flesh and skin,"
k’elles ne copent et oevrent la plaie devant la soudure;	for they would cut and open up the wound before stitching.
et puis cope les chiés des aguilles, qu’elles ne blecent lou malaide au dormir,	"Then clip the heads of the needles so that they do not prick the sick person while sleeping,"
et i met tentes ou drapelz au chiés des aguilles por mues tenir,	"And you should put caps or cloths on the heads of the needles to prevent movement."
et les laisse tant que li plaie soit soudee;	"Leave them until the wound is healed,"
et ceste maniere de costure as aguilles est plus covenauble en petites plaies,	"And this method of stitching with needles is more suitable for small wounds,"
car il i soffist une aguille ou .ij.	For it requires only one or two needles
Li seconde costure si est commune,	The second suture is common,
et est que tu assemble les .ij. chiés dou cuir et les .ij. chiés dou syfac ensamble a une aguille ou il ait .i. fort fil moien;	And you shall assemble the two bones of the skin and the two bones of the hip together with one needle having a medium strong thread.
et quant tu avras perciez ces chiez toz .iiij. ensamble,	and when you have pierced all four of these bones together,
si ramoinne l’aguille a la partie ou tu as encomenciet, en la maniere c’on cout les dras;	"Then reset the needle at the point where you began, as one cuts cloth."
et met d’espaice entre chescune costure la grossece d’un menor doi;	"And space each stitch the thickness of a middle finger;
ceste costure sevent li home,	"This seam seals the limb,"
et je cousi une plaie c’uns hons avoit ou ventre,	"I sewed a wound that a man had in his belly,"
qui estoit navrez d’un coutel,	"who was wounded by a knife,"
et estoit li plaie plus d’une palme de grant,	"And the wound was more than a palm's breadth wide,"
et issoit des intestines bien .ij. palmes de grant,	"and it showed more than two palms' worth of intestines."
et estoit li plaie enmi le ventre.	"The wound was in his belly."
Je li ramenai l’intestine puis k’il ot esteit .xxiiij. houres fuer,	"I reset the intestine twenty-four hours after it had been dislocated,"
et fut li plaie soudee jusc’a .xv. jors, et le curai, et fut sanez.	"And the wound healed up to fifteen days, and I treated it, and he recovered."
Et li mire l’avoient jugiet qu’il morroit, et ce fut miracle;	"And the physicians had judged that he would die, but this was a miracle;"
et ne le curai mie d’oignement, car je estoie en .i. leu ou on n’en trovoit point, ne nule medicines;	"and I did not treat him with ointments, for there were none available in the place where we were, nor any medicine."
et metoie sens plus sus la plaie coton viel .ij. fois le jor, et le lavoie d’aigue de miel tant qu’il fut sanez.	"I simply put on a little cotton twice a day and washed him with honey water until he healed."
Or vos dirai les .ij. propres manieres de cousture:	"Now I will tell you the two proper methods of suturing:"
pren l’aguille, et la boute des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens;	"Take the needle and pass it from the outside to the inside."
quant elle a perciet le keur de droit en droit, si lai le chief dou siphac ou cousteit ou tu as bouteit l’aguille,	"When it has pierced through the heart straight on, then let go of the needle's end or the point where you inserted the needle,"
et la fai percier d’autre part des la partie dedens jusc’a celi defuer;	"and make it pierce again from inside to outside."
et li entendemens de ceste costure si est que tu cous ausi com li peletier font les pelz,	"And the purpose of this suturing method is that you stitch as skinners sew hides,"
et que tu laisses une fois le syfac d’une part, et le reprent d’autre, tant que li costure soit toute acomplie.	"so that once you release the needle on one side, you pick it up again on the other, until the entire stitch is complete."
Li seconde maniere de costure, que Galiens dist proprement,	"The second method of suturing, which Galen describes correctly,"
si est si com aucun font, qui assemblent les .ij. parties ensamble naturelment,	"is to approximate the two parts naturally together,"
et apploient l’un des chief dou syfac a l’autre chief, en teil maniere:	"and press one end of the needle against the other, like this:"
fiche une aguille ou chief dou mirach prochiene, et fai percier celui leu soulement,	"insert a needle close by and pierce only that spot,"
et laisse les .ij. chiés dou syfac;	"and leave both ends of the needles."
puis torne l’aguille, et la fai percier des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens,	"then turn the needle and pass it from outside to inside,"
as .ij. chiés dou syfac;	"so that both ends of the needles are inside,"
puis fai percier l’un et l’autre des la partie defuers jusc’a celi dedens, en .ij. autres chiés dou mirach que sont on l’autre costeit;	"then pierce both sides from outside to inside in two other nearby spots that are opposite each other."
et c’est li muedre maniere de costure et li plus commune.	"And this is the second and most common method of suturing."
Galiens si dist ceste parolle, et aucun le tesmoignent,	"Galen said this, and some confirm it,"
c’on doit coudre le ventre a .ij. aguilles, ou il ait fil en chescune;	"That one should suture the belly with two needles, each having thread."
et doit on bouter l’une aguille d’une part, et l’autre d’autre, en la maniere de ces qui cousent corroies;	"And one must insert one needle on this side and the other on that side, like those who sew hides:"
et saiches que quant li routure est enmi lou ventre,	"And know that when a wound is inside the belly,"
si est li cousture plus griez que des autres leus dou ventre.	"the stitching is tighter than in other parts of the belly."
Li jugemens de la plaie si est telz com li jugemens des autres plaies:	"The judgment of wounds is such as for other wounds:"
et est que quant tu trueves la plaie fresche a tout son sanc, ainsois que li ars l’ait muee,	"And that when you find the wound fresh and full of blood before it has been moved,"
si remet arer l’intestine, et lou cout; puis met sus la poudre enjanrant char,	"then quickly remove the intestines and the cut, then apply powdered gum around the edges."
et se li ars l’ait muee, si met sus aucun oignement que soit present, tant que li plaie bowe;	"If it has been moved, then apply some ointment that is available until the wound closes."
et chicent li fil, et soient soudez li sifac, et li mirach;	"And cut the thread and tie the needle ends and edges."
puis cure la plaie si com les autres, tant qu’il soit sanez;	"Then treat the wound as others, until it heals."
et se tu n’as medicines, si met sus, tantost qu’ele comance a giter bowe, coton viel,	"And if you don't have medicines, then apply cotton wool immediately when it starts to close,"
et le remue .ij. fois le jor tant k’il soit sanez.	"and change it twice a day until it heals."
Car tu n’as mestier d’autre medicine en plusors dispositions cant les plaies sont simples;	"For in many cases where wounds are simple, you don't need any other medicine besides cotton wool."
et se tu doutes que li plaie ne faice communiteit as membres principelz,	"And if you suspect that the wound does not communicate with the main organs,"
si covient ke tu moilles lainne legiere en oile de tempree chalor, ou en oile roset,	"then it is necessary to moisten a light linen cloth in warm oil of wild thyme or rose oil,"
et la met entor les angres, et desoz les asselles;	"and apply it around the angles and under the armpits;"
et s’il sent dolor ou porriture en bouelz, et maintes fois avient,	"And if there is pain or putrefaction in the bowels, which often happens,"
si les clisterize de vin noir tede, et meismement se li porriture vient jusc’a l’intestine;	"then apply black wine enemas and especially if the putrefaction reaches the intestines."
et le perce dedens, et saiches que quant c’est li gros intestines, si est plus legier a saner que li petis.	"And pierce it inside, and know that when it is the large intestine, it is easier to heal than the small one."
Li intestine qui est apelez «jeun» ne puet saner quant il est navrez,	"The intestine called 'jejunum' cannot heal when it is wounded,"
et c’est por la planteit des voinnes que i sont, et por la subtiliteit de tout le cors, et l’aprochement de sa nature des ners.	"And this is because of the thinness of its walls and the delicacy of all the body and its proximity to the nerves."
Et si li zirbe saut de la plaie, si le remet arrier ausi com l’intestine, tandis qu’il est fres;	"If the spleen jumps out of the wound, then put it back in as quickly as possible, while still fresh,"
et s’il est vielz et devenus vers ou noir, si covient que tu lies le leu qui est noir, que decorremens de sanc n’i viegne,	"And if it is old and become black or full of worms, then tie the spot that is black so that no blood flows there,"
car il i a voinnes et arteres;	For there are veins and arteries;
puis cope ceu qui est entre le liien,	Then cut what is between the ligaments,
et met les .ij. chiés pendans des la partie desoz la plaie jusque defuer por aligier l’estraction quant li zirbes chiet, et li plaie bowe.	and put the two bones that are below the wound outwards until they fall on either side of the wound to facilitate extraction when the joint drops, and let the wound gape.
de la routure dou boueil	from dislocation of the eyeball
Quant li intestine est rons, et li plaie est petite,	When the intestines are torn and the wound is small,
si la puet on restorer en aucuns homes,	can it be restored in any way?
por ceu que je vis que uns hons fut navrez ou ventre d’une lance;	for I have seen that a man was wounded in the belly with a lance;
et estoit li plaie au destre de l’estomac,	and the wound was on the right side of the stomach,
et fut envillie et devint fistule, et en issoit li egestion et li ventositez;	And it was inflamed and became a fistula, and the evacuation and wind escaped through it.
je i mis cure selonc ceu que je poi, et ne cessai de subtilier tant qu’il fut sanez, et li leus soudez.	I applied treatment according to what I could, and did not cease until he was healed, and the joints were sound.
Et quant je le vis souder, je doutai que li malaides n’eust mal en son ventre;	And when I saw him healed, I doubted that the patient might still have an illness in his belly;
et il n’i ot point de mal, mais demora en millors dispositions, et menjans et bevans;	and there was no harm, but it remained in better positions, eating and drinking;
et dirent aucun experimentors que quant il a petite plaie en l’intestine, qu’il doit estre liiez en teil maniere:	and some experts said that when there is a small wound in the intestines, it should be tied in this manner:
pren fremis a grans testes, puis assemble les levres de la plaie,	Take fresh large testicles, then gather the edges of the wound,
et quant li fremis ait overte la bouche, si la met sus les .ij. levres,	"When the tremor has opened its mouth, place it over the two lips."
si qu’elle estraigne sa bouche sus;	"So that she pulls her mouth away."
et puis li cope la teste, et ce se tient si qu’il ne puet desliier,	"And then he cuts off the head, and this holds so that it cannot be loosened,"
puis met .i. autre fremit aprés en celle maniere que devant, tant que li plaie soit toute porprise;	"Then puts another bandage afterwards in the same manner as before until the wound is entirely covered;"
et cout la plaie.	"And sew up the wound."
Cil chief si s’aerdent en l’intestine, et ne vient nulle nuisance au malaide,	"This head enters into the intestines and causes no harm to the patient,"
et se puet on liier l’intestine d’un fil subtil qui est copez de l’intestine d’une beste,	"and one can tie the intestine with a fine thread which has been cut from an animal's intestine,"
en teil maniere:	"in this manner:"
pren le chief de cest fil d’intestine que soit mout descharnez,	"Take the head of this intestinal thread that is very skinned,"
et puis lie au chief de cest fil .i. fil de lin subtil tort,	"And then tie to the head of this thread a fine twisted linen thread,"
puis boute le fil en l’aguille, et en cout l’intestine, et le ramoinne en la routure;	"then pass the thread through the needle and sew up the intestine and draw it back into its opening;"
et ceste maniere de costure de fremis nen est fuers que selonc la voie de fiance et d’esperance;	"And this manner of sewing with bandages is not foreign to those who seek confidence and hope."
et se li plaie est grans et large, meismement quant elle est en l’un des grailes intestines, si n’i a engien ne santeit, fuer que subtiliteit.	"But if the wound is large and wide, especially when it is in one of the main intestines, there is no device nor remedy except for subtlety."
de fistule ou qu’ele soit	"of fistula wherever it may be"
Saiches que toute plaie ou aposteme, quant il enveillist, si est apelee universement «fistule»,	"Know that every wound or abscess, when it grows old, is universally called a 'fistula',"
et meismement quant elle est chevee et rent bowe.	"And especially when it is healed and returns inside."
Et fistule est selonc la verteit nodation fautree dure et blainche, ou on ne sent dolor,	"A fistula is, according to its true nature, a hard and white knot or node, where no pain is felt,"
et est ausi chevee com li penne d’un oiseil;	"And its head is as sharp as a bird's feather;"
et aucune fois en saut clere bowe, et autre fois espesse;	"Sometimes it jumps clear and straight; other times it is thick;"
aucune fois poc, et autre fois assez;	"Sometimes soft, sometimes sufficient;"
et je en ai jai parleit en la division des plaies, que toute plaie que n’est sanee, et il n’i a char,	"I have spoken of this in the section on wounds, that any wound which is not clean and lacks flesh,"
ce n’est fuers que par une des .viiij. causes:	"is only so by one of the eight causes:"
c’est a savoir, par la petitece dou sanc ou cors;	"That is to say, due to the smallness of blood or body;"
ou por sa malice;	"or because of its wickedness;"
ou por ceu qu’il i a char dure dedens, et sus les levres, que n’i laisse naistre char;	"or because there is hard flesh within and on the lips, which prevents flesh from growing;"
ou il i a trop de bowe;	"or if there is too much bow;"
ou li leus est porris, et li matiere est de male qualiteit;	"or if the wound is closed up, and the material is of poor quality;"
ou li medicine n’est mie bone en la cure;	"or if the medicine used for treatment was not good;"
ou por ceu que li corruption est maniere de pestilence;	"or because the corruption is a matter of pestilence;"
ou por la proprieteit en la region est tardive li digestion, et tarde li santeit, et enflee par nature;	"or because the property in that region has delayed digestion and healing, and it naturally tends towards inflammation."
ou il i a voinnes ou os:	"or if there are veins or bones present;"
et j’ai ja mostreit toutes ces causes, et les signes, et les cures de medicines en la division.	"I have already shown all these causes, signs, and medicinal treatments in the relevant section."
Or covient que je te faice a savoir la cure de fistule qui est faite par oevre de mains.	"Now I must tell you about the treatment of fistula which is done by manual work."
Saiches que fistule avient en tous membres dou cors;	"You should know that fistulas occur in all parts of the body;"
car il i a fistules que vienent as grans voines, et as arteres, et as ners,	"for there are fistulas which come from large veins and arteries and nerves,"
ou au syfac, ou a l’intestine, ou a la vessie, ou a aucunes des costes,	"or from the sinews, intestines, bladder, or ribs;"
ou a l’espinee dou dos, ou a aucune jointe des mains ou des piez;	"or from the spine of the back, or any joint of the hands or feet."
et si a teil que vient a la proprieteit dou membre principeil, et as semblans leus.	"And sometimes it comes to the property of the main member and similar places."
Et toutes les fistules que sont de ceste maniere sont de grief sanation, et n’i a fors que labour, et ignorance;	"All such fistulas are difficult to heal, and there is only labor involved in their treatment, along with ignorance;"
et se il i a aucune fistule que ne veigne mie jusc’a leu que j’ai dit, et tu as fiance de la cure,	"And if there is any fistula that does not reach the places I have mentioned, you can be confident about its treatment,"
et tu la vues conoistre, si pren une tente d’arain ou de fer, se li fistule est droite, si la quier;	"And you will recognize it; so take an awl of iron or bronze, and if the fistula is straight, bore into it;"
et se li fistule est torte, si la cerche d’une subtil tente de plonc,	"and if the fistula is curved, search for it with a thin lead probe."
car li plons se ploie mues entor la tortuositeit;	"because lead will bend more easily around the curvature;"
et se li fistule a mains pertus et tu ne la pues mie bien cerchier par tentes,	"And if the fistula has many perforations and you cannot search for it well with probes,"
si la clisterize par l’un des pertus,	"then irrigate it through one of the perforations."
car la moistors si cort d’un pertus a autre, et la mundifie;	"because moisture will flow from one perforation to another and cleanse them;"
puis la quier saigement a ton pooir, que tu conoisses s’il i a os ou nerf, et est chevee em parfont,	"then probe gently so that you know if there is bone or nerve present, and how deep it goes."
et demande bien au malaide de la dolor qu’il sent au presser de ta main, et le leu ou il la sent;	"And ask the patient carefully about the pain they feel when your hand presses on them, and where they feel it."
et quant tu savras vraiement le leu ou elle est, et s’elle est loing de jointure, ou de nerf, ou d’artere ou de voine,	"and once you know exactly where the fistula is located, and if it is far from a joint or nerve, artery, or vein,"
ou en aucuns des leus que je t’ai dit, si la cope selonc ceu que je t’ai dit,	"then cut into it according to what I have told you."
et oste fuer la fautreure et les chars corrumpues que sont dedens;	"And remove the breach and corrupted tissue that is inside;"
et puis la cure tant qu’elle soit sanee,	"And then treat it until it is healed;"
